---
title: "Network Manager is a unholy abomination of the Devil!"
date: 2011-02-27
forum: General Help
---

### Post by highspider on 2011-02-27
Yes, Network Manager is the Devil.

what happened. 
So every one on the forums keeps ranting and raving about how there are no login themes for the new GDM2.X version of Ubuntu (and the default blows) sure you can change the background pic with 
sudo -u gdm gconftool-2 --set --type string --set /desktop/gnome/background/picture_filename /dir/mypic.jpg
 but the lame nutz login window blows. so you begin hacking the greeter .UI which is more like a .XML  while making your own dragon login; however, you find the gtk+ programs in software are too out dated to make it cool. so you upgrade your libglib2 2.24.1, as dependent, to your own tar.gz source made in package vers 2.28.0.  and forget to update the dev version also.  you f-up and reboot only to find linux crashes to tty1 mode and your stuck with only a console and NO INTERNET.  bummer 

first you sprinkly holy water on network manger and recite a few catholic versus of the bible. 
next you edit the /etc/networking/network with
```

auto eth0
iface eth0 inet static
address 192.168.0.10
gateway 192.168.0.1
netmask 255.255.255.0
broadcast 192.168.0.255

```edit the /etc/resolv.conf
```
nameserver 192.168.0.1
```ping Google (yes allways Google for pinging just cuz everybody does google pings and don't want to be different.)
```

Devil@hell.com$ ping www.google.com
PING www.l.google.com (74.125.53.99) 56(84) bytes of data.
64 bytes from pw-in-f99.1e100.net (74.125.53.99): icmp_seq=1 ttl=53 time=48.5 ms

```you do your happy dance while squeaking out a hi-pitched girlishly yeess and quickly look over should to make sure no one say or heard you.

now you can type 
```

aptitude

```from the command line and fix your error with internet to link the old packages YEAH! and of course posting about it on the forums because well I have no life. I guess i'm just naturally unlikeable.

seriously this just happened to me!!! 

  And if i where to have depended on the unholy abominations of network manager i would have never      been able to do this from the console.

If you really read all this please comment.

### Post by hugmenot on 2011-04-01
Look son. Before you venture to break your system libraries haphazardly it /might/ be a good idea to find out first how to restore everything, including your networking.

```
nmcli con list
nmcli con up id Ethernet
```

It’s not magic. Neither black nor white magic. Just learn to study the man scrolls.
